Maddie Keyser '15 is an English & German double major who spent time researching the Tolkein collection in Cushing Library. Here's how she described that experience:\n\n\"The summer of my freshman year I applied for an internship at Cushing Memorial Library and Archives. I work with Dr. Mitchell and go through his collection of books from the Garnett family. I make notes on all the inscriptions, bookplates, newspaper articles, photos that are in the books and make notes on any differences in bindings, book jackets, etc. among different editions of the same book. I also conducted my own research project which will culminate in my senior thesis for the English Honors Program using sixteen philological books (in German) and notes that belonged to J.R.R. Tolkien. These books are books from his personal library that he used in his academic work as a professor at Oxford University. I encourage you to share suicide prevention resources with your Facebook community and your student community. Talking openly about suicide is important to raising awareness, educating, and reducing the stigma of suicide. Some organizations that provide excellent suicide awareness information are: The American Foundation for Suicide Prevention (http://www.afsp.org/) and To Write Love on her Arms (http://www.twloha.com/) which focuses on suicide prevention on college campuses. \r\n\r\nAs students return, it is important to be open and honest about the cause of Dr. Aune's death as hiding the fact that he died by suicide furthers the stigma of suicide and can cause students (or faculty and staff) to ignore warning signs (in themselves or others) or not seek the help that they may need. Distributing information about warning signs for suicide, suicide hotlines, and coping resources is crucial to preventing suicide and keeping a healthy student body. \r\n\r\nI lost one of my best friends to suicide 2 years ago and am passionate about the necessity to have an open and honest dialog about suicide.\r\n\r\nBest, \r\n\r\nJennifer McNichols\r\n\r\n", "icon": "https://fbstatic-a.akamaihd.net/rsrc.php/v2/yD/r/aS8ecmYRys0.gif", "type": "link", "id": "64396601157_111744529001275", "status_type": "shared_story", "description": "The American Foundation for Suicide Prevention (AFSP)   is the leading national not-for-profit organization   exclusively dedicated to understanding and preventing   suicide through research, education and advocacy, and   to reaching out to people with mental disorders and   those impacted by suicid..."}
